Source Code

This source code is very close to the Apollo Guidance Computer software for the Apollo 13 Lunar module. This revision of the Luminary 131 program is from December of 1969, whereas there was a later revision in January of 1970, and still another revision in February, which is the code that flew on the mission. As far as this transcription is concerned, it was originally from a copy made in 1991 of a printout from the collection of AGC developer Don Eyles for collector David Craig. It was subsequently scanned by Gary Neff, reprocessed for online presentation at the now-discontinued History of Recent Science and Technology (HRST) website of MIT's Dibner Institute (the full-quality scans being discarded in the process), and finally transcribed by Ron Burkey for the Virtual AGC Project. Although a high-quality replacement scan for a completely illegible page was later provided by Gary Neff, the reduced legibility of the reprocessed HRST posting nevertheless caused many errors to be introduced into the transcription. Accordingly, a second scan of the same physical printout was made in 2017 for the Virtual AGC Project's collection at the Internet Archive, and used to correct the transcription errors. All of the scanned materials mentioned, as well as other Luminary 131 related material, are available online. Don Eyles apprently made additional hand-written notes in printout between 1991 and 2017, so the two scans are not identical in that respect. The page-headings in the printout read, in part:
	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date the printout was made, not the date on which the program revision was released, although these happen to be very close together. 

021000,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021001,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021002,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
021003,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
021004,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13.
021005,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
021006,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
021007,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
021008,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
021009,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 496-618
021010,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021011,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021012,000014:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 05/15/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.
021013,000015:                                                                                                  ##              12/01/03 RSB.   Entered/corrected the previously-missing code from
021014,000016:                                                                                                  ##                              the bottom of p. 595 using a replacement scan
021015,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              provided by Gary Neff.
021016,000018:                                                                                                  ##              05/14/05 RSB    Corrected website reference above.

021027,000029:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021028,000030: 
021029,000031:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021030,000032: 
021031,000033:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021032,000034:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021033,000035: 
021034,000036:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021035,000037: 
021036,000038:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021037,000039:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021038,000040:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021039,000041:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021040,000042: 
021041,000043:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021042,000044: 
021043,000045:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021044,000046: 
021045,000047:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021046,000048: 
021047,000049:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021048,000050:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021049,000051:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021050,000052:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021051,000053:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021052,000054:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021053,000055:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021054,000056:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021055,000057:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021056,000058:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021057,000059: 
021058,000060:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021059,000061: 
021060,000062:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021061,000063:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021062,000064: 
021063,000065:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021064,000066: 
021065,000067:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021066,000068: 
021067,000069:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021068,000070: 
021069,000071:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021070,000072: 
021071,000073:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021072,000074: 
021073,000075:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021074,000076: 
021075,000077:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021076,000078: 
021077,000079:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021078,000080: 
021079,000081:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021080,000082: 
021081,000083: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021082,000084: 
021083,000085: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021084,000086: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021085,000087: 24,2000                                           BANK

021495,000497:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021496,000498: 
021497,000499:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021498,000500:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021499,000501:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021500,000502: 
021501,000503:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021502,000504: 
021503,000505:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021504,000506:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021505,000507:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021506,000508:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021507,000509: 
021508,000510:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021509,000511: 
021510,000512:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021511,000513: 
021512,000514:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021513,000515: 
021514,000516:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP
021515,000517:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      ENDOFJOB
021516,000518:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)                     WAITLIST
021517,000519:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC
021518,000520: 
021519,000521:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -

021521,000523:                                                                                                  #        P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021522,000524:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021584,000586:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021585,000587:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021586,000588: 
021587,000589:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021588,000590:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021589,000591: 
021590,000592:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021591,000593: 
021592,000594:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021593,000595:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021594,000596: 
021595,000597:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021596,000598: 
021597,000599:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021598,000600:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021599,000601: 
021600,000602:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021601,000603: 
021602,000604:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021603,000605:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021604,000606:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021605,000607: 
021606,000608:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021607,000609: 
021608,000610:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA

Page 512 

021804,000806:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021805,000807:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021806,000808: 
021807,000809:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021808,000810:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021809,000811: 
021810,000812:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021811,000813: 
021812,000814:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021813,000815:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021814,000816: 
021815,000817:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021816,000818: 
021817,000819:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021818,000820:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021819,000821: 
021820,000822:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021821,000823: 
021822,000824:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021823,000825:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021824,000826:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021825,000827:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021826,000828: 
021827,000829:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021828,000830:                                                                                                  #        
021829,000831:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021830,000832:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021831,000833: 
021832,000834:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021833,000835: 
021834,000836:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021835,000837:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021836,000838:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021837,000839: 
021838,000840:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021839,000841: 
021840,000842:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021841,000843: 
021842,000844:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021843,000845: 
021844,000846:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021845,000847: 
021846,000848:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021847,000849: 
021848,000850:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021849,000851: 
021850,000852:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021851,000853: 
021852,000854:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRSESSM
021853,000855: 
021854,000856: 24,2675  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021855,000857: 24,2675                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
021856,000858: 24,2675           44736        R21LEM             CS       BIT14                                 #  REMOVE RR SELF TRACK ENABLE
021857,000859: 24,2676           00006                           EXTEND                                         
021858,000860: 24,2677           03012                           WAND     CHAN12

022030,001032:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022031,001033:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022032,001034: 
022033,001035:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022034,001036:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022035,001037: 
022036,001038:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022037,001039: 
022038,001040:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022039,001041: 
022040,001042:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022041,001043: 
022042,001044:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022043,001045: 
022044,001046:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022045,001047: 
022046,001048:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022047,001049:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022048,001050: 
022049,001051:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022050,001052: 
022051,001053:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022052,001054:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022053,001055:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022054,001056: 
022055,001057:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022056,001058: 
022057,001059:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022058,001060: 
022059,001061:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022060,001062: 
022061,001063:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022062,001064: 
022063,001065:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022064,001066: 
022065,001067:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
022066,001068: 
022067,001069: 24,3137     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022068,001070: 24,3137                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022069,001071: 24,3137           05504        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022070,001072: 24,3140           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
022071,001073: 24,3141           00004                           INHINT                                         
022072,001074: 24,3142           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
022073,001075: 24,3143           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
022074,001076: 24,3144           00003                           RELINT                                         
022075,001077: 24,3145           34736        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
022076,001078: 24,3146           00006                           EXTEND

022078,001080: 24,3150           33207                           CAF      OCT205                                
022079,001081: 24,3151           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022080,001082: 24,3152           20624                           CADR     GOPERF1                               
022081,001083: 24,3153           03200                           TC       R23LEM2                               #  TERMINATE

022114,001116:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022115,001117:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022116,001118: 
022117,001119:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022118,001120:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022119,001121: 
022120,001122:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022121,001123: 
022122,001124:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022123,001125:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022124,001126:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022125,001127: 
022126,001128:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022127,001129: 
022128,001130:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022129,001131:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022130,001132:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022131,001133:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022132,001134: 
022133,001135:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022134,001136: 
022135,001137:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022136,001138:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022137,001139:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022138,001140: 
022139,001141:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022140,001142: 
022141,001143:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022142,001144:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022143,001145:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022144,001146: 
022145,001147:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022146,001148: 
022147,001149:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022148,001150: 
022149,001151:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022150,001152: 
022151,001153:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022152,001154: 
022153,001155:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022154,001156: 
022155,001157:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022156,001158: 
022157,001159:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022158,001160: 
022159,001161:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022160,001162: 
022161,001163: 24,3210  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022162,001164: 24,3210                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022163,001165: 24,3210           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022164,001166: 24,3211           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022165,001167: 24,3212           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022166,001168: 24,3213           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022167,001169: 24,3214           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022168,001170: 24,3215           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022169,001171: 24,3216           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022170,001172: 24,3217           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022171,001173: 24,3220           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022172,001174: 24,3221           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022173,001175: 24,3222           33255                           CAF      V16N80                                
022174,001176: 24,3223           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022175,001177: 24,3224           20505                           CADR     PRIODSPR                              
022176,001178: 24,3225           06025                           TC       GOTOV56                               
022177,001179: 24,3226           03232                           TC       R24END                                #  PROCEED EXIT R24 TO P20LEM1
022178,001180: 
022179,001181: 24,3227           03236                           TC       R24LEM3                               #  RECYCLE - CALL R61 TO MANEUVER S/C

022222,001224: 24,3252           34755        R24LEM4            CAF      ZERO                                  #  ZERO OUT RADCADR (WHICH WAS SET BY
022223,001225: 24,3253           55303                           TS       RADCADR                               #  ENDRADAR WHEN DESIGNATE STOPPED) SO THAT
022224,001226:                                                                                                  #  RRDESSM WILL RETURN TO CALLER
022225,001227: 24,3254           03220                           TC       R24LEM2                               #  AND GO BACK TO PUT UP V16 N80 DISPLAY

022230,001232:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022231,001233:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

022459,001461:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022460,001462: 
022461,001463:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022462,001464: 
022463,001465:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022464,001466:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022465,001467:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022466,001468:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022467,001469:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022468,001470: 
022469,001471:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022470,001472:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022471,001473:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022472,001474:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022473,001475: 
022474,001476:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022475,001477:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022476,001478:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022477,001479:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022478,001480:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022479,001481: 
022480,001482:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022481,001483: 
022482,001484:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022483,001485:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022484,001486: 
022485,001487:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022486,001488: 
022487,001489:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022488,001490:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022489,001491:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022490,001492: 
022491,001493:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022492,001494: 
022493,001495:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022494,001496: 
022495,001497:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022496,001498: 
022497,001499:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022498,001500:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)

022543,001545:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                 . IF EITHER:
022544,001546: 
022545,001547:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022546,001548:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.              HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022547,001549:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022548,001550:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022549,001551:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022550,001552:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022551,001553:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022552,001554:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022553,001555:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022554,001556:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022555,001557:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022556,001558:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022557,001559:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022558,001560:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022559,001561:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022560,001562:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU'S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022561,001563:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022562,001564:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022563,001565:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022564,001566:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022565,001567: 
022566,001568:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:

022615,001617:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022616,001618: 
022617,001619:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022618,001620: 
022619,001621:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022620,001622:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022621,001623:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022622,001624:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022623,001625:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022624,001626:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022625,001627:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022626,001628:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022627,001629:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022628,001630:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022629,001631:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022630,001632:                                                                                                  #        TC TASKOVER.
022631,001633: 
022632,001634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022633,001635:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022634,001636:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022635,001637: 
022636,001638:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022637,001639: 
022638,001640:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022639,001641: 
022640,001642:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022641,001643: 
022642,001644:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022643,001645:                                                                                                  #        
022644,001646:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022645,001647: 
022646,001648:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022647,001649: 
022648,001650:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022649,001651: 
022650,001652: 24,3256                                           BANK     24                                    
022651,001653: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022652,001654: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022653,001655: 
022654,001656: 25,2073  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

022664,001666:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022665,001667: 
022666,001668:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022667,001669: 
022668,001670:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022669,001671:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022670,001672:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022671,001673:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022672,001674:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022673,001675:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022674,001676:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU'S
022675,001677:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022676,001678:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022677,001679:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022678,001680:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022679,001681:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022680,001682:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022681,001683:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022682,001684:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022683,001685: 
022684,001686:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022685,001687: 
022686,001688:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022687,001689: 
022688,001690:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022689,001691: 
022690,001692:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022691,001693: 
022692,001694:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022693,001695: 
022694,001696:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022695,001697: 
022696,001698:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022697,001699: 
022698,001700:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022699,001701: 
022700,001702: 25,2102           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
022701,001703: 25,2103           23312                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
022702,001704: 25,2104           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
022703,001705: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022704,001706: 25,2106           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU

022741,001743:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022742,001744: 
022743,001745:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022744,001746: 
022745,001747:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022746,001748:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022747,001749:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022748,001750:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022749,001751:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022750,001752:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022751,001753:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022752,001754:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022753,001755:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022754,001756:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022755,001757:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022756,001758:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022757,001759:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022758,001760:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022759,001761:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022760,001762:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022761,001763:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022762,001764:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022763,001765:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022764,001766:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022765,001767:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022766,001768:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022767,001769: 
022768,001770:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022769,001771: 
022770,001772:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022771,001773:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022772,001774: 
022773,001775:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022774,001776: 
022775,001777:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022776,001778: 
022777,001779:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022778,001780: 
022779,001781:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022780,001782: 
022781,001783:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022782,001784: 
022783,001785:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022784,001786: 
022785,001787:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022786,001788: 
022787,001789:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022788,001790: 
022789,001791: 25,2140           02167        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022790,001792:

022834,001836:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022835,001837: 
022836,001838:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022837,001839:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022838,001840:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022839,001841:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022840,001842:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022841,001843:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022842,001844:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022843,001845:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022844,001846:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022845,001847:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022846,001848:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022847,001849:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022848,001850:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022849,001851:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022850,001852:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022851,001853:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022852,001854:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022853,001855:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022854,001856:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022855,001857:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022856,001858: 
022857,001859:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022858,001860: 
022859,001861:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022860,001862:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022861,001863:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022862,001864:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022863,001865: 
022864,001866:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022865,001867: 
022866,001868:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022867,001869: 
022868,001870:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022869,001871: 
022870,001872:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022871,001873: 
022872,001874:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022873,001875:

022875,001877:

022930,001932:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022931,001933: 
022932,001934:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022933,001935: 
022934,001936:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022935,001937:                                                                                                  #        RRMANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022936,001938:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022937,001939:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022938,001940:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022939,001941:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022940,001942:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022941,001943:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022942,001944:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022943,001945:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022944,001946:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022945,001947:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022946,001948:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022947,001949:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022948,001950: 
022949,001951:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022950,001952:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022951,001953:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022952,001954:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022953,001955:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022954,001956: 
022955,001957:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022956,001958: 
022957,001959:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022958,001960: 
022959,001961:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022960,001962: 
022961,001963:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
022962,001964: 
022963,001965:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022964,001966: 
022965,001967:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022966,001968: 
022967,001969:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022968,001970: 
022969,001971:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_ REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
022970,001972:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)
022971,001973:                                                                                                  #        L+1 (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)

023022,002024:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023023,002025: 
023024,002026:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023025,002027: 
023026,002028:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023027,002029:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023028,002030:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023029,002031:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023030,002032:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023031,002033:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023032,002034:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023033,002035:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023034,002036:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023035,002037:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023036,002038:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023037,002039:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023038,002040:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023039,002041: 
023040,002042:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023041,002043:                                                                                                  #        
023042,002044:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023043,002045:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023048,002050:                                                                                                  #        (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENAGLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
