023132,002134:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023133,002135: 
023134,002136:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023135,002137: 
023136,002138:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023137,002139:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023138,002140:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023139,002141:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023140,002142:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023141,002143:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023142,002144:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023143,002145:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023144,002146:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023145,002147:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023146,002148:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023147,002149:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023148,002150:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023149,002151:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023150,002152:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023151,002153:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023152,002154:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023153,002155:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023154,002156:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023155,002157:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023156,002158:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023157,002159:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023158,002160: 
023159,002161:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023160,002162: 
023161,002163:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023162,002164:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023163,002165:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023164,002166:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023165,002167: 
023166,002168:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023167,002169: 
023168,002170:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023169,002171: 
023170,002172:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023171,002173: 
023172,002174:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023173,002175:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023174,002176: 
023175,002177:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023176,002178: 
023177,002179:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023178,002180: 
023179,002181:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023180,002182: 
023181,002183:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023182,002184:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023183,002185:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                 CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
023184,002186:

023222,002224:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023223,002225: 
023224,002226:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023225,002227:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023226,002228:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023227,002229:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023228,002230:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023229,002231:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023230,002232:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023231,002233:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023232,002234:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023233,002235:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023234,002236:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023235,002237:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023236,002238:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023237,002239:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023238,002240:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023239,002241:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023240,002242:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023241,002243:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023242,002244:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023243,002245:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023244,002246:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.

023395,002397:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023396,002398: 
023397,002399:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023398,002400:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023399,002401:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023400,002402:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023401,002403:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023402,002404:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023403,002405:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023404,002406:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023405,002407:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023406,002408:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023407,002409:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023408,002410:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023409,002411:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023410,002412:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023411,002413:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023412,002414:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023413,002415:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023414,002416:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023415,002417:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023416,002418:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023417,002419:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023418,002420:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023419,002421:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023420,002422:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023421,002423:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023422,002424:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023423,002425: 
023424,002426:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023425,002427: 
023426,002428:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023427,002429:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023428,002430:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023429,002431: 
023430,002432:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023431,002433:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023432,002434: 
023433,002435:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023434,002436:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDMAC
023435,002437: 
023436,002438:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023437,002439: 
023438,002440:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023439,002441:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023440,002442: 
023441,002443:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023442,002444:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023443,002445:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023444,002446: 
023445,002447: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023490,002492:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023491,002493: 
023492,002494:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023493,002495: 
023494,002496:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023495,002497:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023496,002498:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023497,002499:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023498,002500:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023499,002501:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023500,002502:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023501,002503:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023502,002504:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023503,002505:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023504,002506:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023505,002507:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023506,002508:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023507,002509:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023508,002510:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023509,002511:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023510,002512:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023511,002513:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023512,002514:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023513,002515:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023514,002516:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023515,002517:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023516,002518:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023517,002519:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023518,002520:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023519,002521:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023520,002522:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023521,002523:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023522,002524:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023523,002525:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023524,002526:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023525,002527:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023526,002528:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023527,002529:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023528,002530:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023529,002531:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023530,002532:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023531,002533: 
023532,002534:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023533,002535: 
023534,002536:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023535,002537: 
023536,002538:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023537,002539: 
023538,002540:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023539,002541:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023540,002542: 
023541,002543:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023542,002544: 
023543,002545:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 552 

023545,002547: 
023546,002548:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023547,002549: 
023548,002550:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023549,002551: 
023550,002552:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023551,002553: 
023552,002554:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023553,002555: 
023554,002556: 25,2646           00006        DODES              EXTEND

023608,002610:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE.  CONVERT THIS TO A
023609,002611:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

023615,002617: 25,2731           40110                           CS       RADMODES                              #  A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES POLARITY OF
023616,002618: 25,2732           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A
023617,002619: 25,2733           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  POSITIVE TORQUE APPLIED TO THE SHAFT
023618,002620: 25,2734           12737                           BZF      +3                                    #  GYRO CAUSES A POSITIVE CHANGE IN THE
023619,002621: 25,2735           31107                           CA       TANG       +1                         #  SHAFT ANGLE.  COMPENSATE FOR THIS SWITCH
023620,002622: 25,2736           12740                           TCF      +2                                    #  BY CHANGING THE POLARITY OF OUR COMMAND.

024227,003229:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION

024231,003233:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.

024356,003358:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024357,003359:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024358,003360: 
024359,003361:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024360,003362:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024361,003363:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024362,003364:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024363,003365:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024364,003366: 
024365,003367:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024366,003368: 
024367,003369:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024368,003370:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024369,003371:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024370,003372:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024371,003373:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024372,003374: 
024373,003375:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024374,003376: 
024375,003377:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024376,003378:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024377,003379:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024378,003380: 
024379,003381:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024380,003382:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024381,003383: 
024382,003384:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024383,003385:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024384,003386: 
024385,003387:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024386,003388:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024387,003389:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024388,003390:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024389,003391:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,ADG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024390,003392:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024391,003393: 
024392,003394:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024393,003395:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 575 

024395,003397:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024396,003398:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024397,003399:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024398,003400: 
024399,003401:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X, A, L, Q, PUSHLIST

024529,003531:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LRS22.2 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 2)

024531,003533: 
024532,003534:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
024533,003535:                                                                                                  #        2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E. THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS

024536,003538:

024538,003540: 
024539,003541:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT - RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO +0 (VIA SWRETURN)
024540,003542: 
024541,003543:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXIT -  RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO 00001 - RADAR LOS NOT WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF LM +Z AXIS
024542,003544:

024544,003546:

024547,003549:                                                                                                  #        RM - RR RANGE, METERS B-29, FROM LRS22.1
024548,003550:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 CHANNEL 31 - INDICATES AUTOPILOT IS IN AUTO MODE
024549,003551: 
024550,003552:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS - A,L,Q MPAC - PUSHLIST AND PUSHLOC ARE NOT CHANGED BY THIS ROUTINE

024580,003582:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024581,003583:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024582,003584:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024583,003585: 
024584,003586:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024585,003587:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024586,003588:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024587,003589:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024588,003590: 
024589,003591:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024590,003592:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024591,003593:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024592,003594:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024593,003595:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024594,003596:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024595,003597:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024596,003598: 
024597,003599:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024598,003600:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024599,003601:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024600,003602: 
024601,003603:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024602,003604:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024603,003605:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024604,003606:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024605,003607:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024606,003608:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024607,003609: 
024608,003610:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024609,003611:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024610,003612:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024611,003613:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024612,003614:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024613,003615:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024614,003616:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024615,003617:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024616,003618:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024617,003619:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024618,003620:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN ACG
024619,003621:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024620,003622:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024621,003623:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024622,003624:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024623,003625: 
024624,003626:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024625,003627:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024626,003628:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

024628,003630:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T

025017,004019: 
025018,004020:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025019,004021:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025020,004022:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025021,004023:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025022,004024: 
025023,004025:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025024,004026:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025025,004027:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025026,004028: 
025027,004029:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025028,004030:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025029,004031:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025030,004032:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025031,004033:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025032,004034:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX

Page 589 

025034,004036: 
025035,004037:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025036,004038:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025037,004039:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
025038,004040:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025039,004041:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025040,004042:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025041,004043:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
025042,004044:

025048,004050: 26,3205           77624                           CALL

025242,004244:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025243,004245:                                                                                                  #  MCD NO  0                     BY P VOLANTE  SDC               DATE 1-15-67
025244,004246: 
025245,004247:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025246,004248: 
025247,004249:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025248,004250:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025249,004251:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025250,004252:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025251,004253: 
025252,004254:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025253,004255: 
025254,004256:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025255,004257: 
025256,004258:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025257,004259:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025258,004260:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025259,004261:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025260,004262:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025261,004263: 
025262,004264:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025263,004265: 
025264,004266:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025265,004267: 
025266,004268:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) - FOR DISPLAY IN R1 -     00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025267,004269:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025268,004270:                                                                                                  #        OMEGAD (SP)   - FOR DISPLAY IN R2 -     ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGNT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025269,004271: 
025270,004272:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025271,004273: 
025272,004274:                                                                                                  #        SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025273,004275:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025274,004276: 
025275,004277:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025276,004278: 
025277,004279:                                                                                                  #        RLMSRCH         UXVECT
025278,004280:                                                                                                  #        VXRLM           UYVECT
025279,004281:                                                                                                  #        LOSDESRD        NSRCHPNT
025280,004282:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD        OMEGAD
025281,004283:                                                                                                  #        MPAC            PUSHLIST
025282,004284: 
025283,004285: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025284,004286: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025285,004287: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025286,004288: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025287,004289: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND

025495,004497:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025496,004498:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025497,004499: 
025498,004500:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025499,004501: 
025500,004502:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025501,004503:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025502,004504:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025503,004505:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025504,004506:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025505,004507:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025506,004508: 
025507,004509:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025508,004510: 
025509,004511:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025510,004512: 
025511,004513:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025512,004514:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025513,004515:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025514,004516:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025515,004517:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025516,004518:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025517,004519: 
025518,004520:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025519,004521: 
025520,004522:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025521,004523: 
025522,004524:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025523,004525:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025524,004526:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025525,004527:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025526,004528:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 600 

025528,004530: 
025529,004531:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025530,004532: 
025531,004533:                                                                                                  #        NCR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025532,004534:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025533,004535:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025534,004536:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025535,004537: 
025536,004538:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025537,004539: 
025538,004540:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)
025539,004541:                                                                                                  #        LOSSM           LOSVDT/4                (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025540,004542:                                                                                                  #        SAVECDUT        OLDESFLG                (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025541,004543:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        READRFLG
025542,004544: 
025543,004545:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025544,004546: 
025545,004547:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025546,004548: 
025547,004549:                                                                                                  #        INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE:  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
025548,004550:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
025549,004551:                                                                                                  #        RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
025550,004552:

025651,004653:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN
025652,004654:                                                                                                  #  START IT UP WHEN THE DATA IS IN PLACE.

025657,004659: 33,2143           52255                           VAD      VSU                                   #        AND ADD THE RESULT TO R(CSM) - R TO GET
025658,004660: 33,2144           01720                                    R(CSM)                                #        AN UP-TO-DATE LOS VECTOR IN SM AXES.

Page 605 

025724,004726:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025725,004727: 
025726,004728:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025727,004729:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025728,004730:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025729,004731:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025730,004732:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025731,004733: 
025732,004734:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025733,004735:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025734,004736: 
025735,004737: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025736,004738: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025737,004739: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025738,004740: 
025739,004741: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025740,004742: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025741,004743: 
025742,004744: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025743,004745: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025744,004746: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025745,004747: 
025746,004748: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025747,004749: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025748,004750: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG
